2026-03-15T18:06:00.2175822Z     float Dist2D(CVector const& a, CVector const& b)
2026-03-15T18:06:00.2176284Z     {
2026-03-15T18:06:00.2176567Z         float dx = a.x - b.x;
2026-03-15T18:06:00.2176931Z         float dy = a.y - b.y;
2026-03-15T18:06:00.2177314Z         return std::sqrtf(dx * dx + dy * dy);
2026-03-15T18:06:00.2177713Z     }

2026-03-15T18:06:00.2180570Z     {

2026-03-15T18:06:00.2181946Z         bool just = curr && !s_prev[vk];

2026-03-15T18:06:00.2182986Z     }

2026-03-15T18:09:45.4844873Z

2026-03-15T18:09:45.4846163Z 
2026-03-15T18:09:45.4846939Z Key insight: The project includes `$(PLUGIN_SDK_DIR)\Plugin_SA\game_sa` which includes all GTA SA game headers. CFont, CHud, etc. should be available there.
2026-03-15T18:09:45.4847843Z 
2026-03-15T18:09:45.4848032Z For rendering in GTA SA, I need to use either:
2026-03-15T18:09:45.4848559Z 1. `CFont::PrintString` for text rendering
2026-03-15T18:09:45.4848894Z 
2026-03-15T18:09:45.4848900Z 
2026-03-15T18:09:45.4849063Z 2. `CSprite2d` for sprite and box rendering
2026-03-15T18:09:45.4849555Z 3. Plugin-sdk's event system for hooking into the render pipeline
2026-03-15T18:09:45.4849924Z 
2026-03-15T18:09:45.4852201Z Looking at the plugin-sdk repository, I can see `CFont.h` has methods like SetScale and SetColor, `CHud.h` handles help messages, and there are specific events like `drawHudEvent` that fire during HUD rendering and `d3dPresent` during Direct3D presentation. Since the plugin-sdk is installed separately and we're working with source code, I should be able to hook into these events directly.
2026-03-15T18:09:45.4854424Z 
2026-03-15T18:09:45.4856035Z The CFont API provides static methods for scaling, coloring, justification, and string width calculation, with PrintString handling the actual text rendering. GTA SA uses a virtual 640x448 screen space that scales to the actual resolution, so I'll need to account for that proportional scaling in the menu positioning.
2026-03-15T18:09:45.4857713Z 
2026-03-15T18:09:45.4862090Z For the menu implementation, I'm reconsidering the approach—while hooking drawHudEvent with CFont::PrintString and GetAsyncKeyState would work, using GTA SA's native menu system through CMessages would be simpler and more consistent with the existing codebase. I need to finalize the menu structure - it'll be straightforward text-based with a header showing the current state, then a list of options with their keybinds, and simple navigation using arrow keys to highlight selections. The layout keeps everything minimal and functional without any decorative elements.
2026-03-15T18:09:45.4865331Z 
2026-03-15T18:09:45.4867450Z Now I'm working through the implementation details for managing multiple recruits with vanilla support - I'll need a periodic scan function to detect new group members and apply the necessary enhancement flags to keep them properly integrated, then handle the vehicle allocation logic by switching between leader car and follow modes depending on whether the player is in a vehicle or on foot.

2026-03-15T18:19:48.6074901Z     67.     if (!veh) return baseSpeed;
2026-03-15T18:19:48.6082592Z     68. 
2026-03-15T18:19:48.6082954Z     69.     float vH    = veh->GetHeading();
2026-03-15T18:19:48.6083307Z     70.     float dH    = targetHeading - vH;
2026-03-15T18:19:48.6083626Z     71.     while (dH >  3.14159f) dH -= 6.28318f;
2026-03-15T18:19:48.6083933Z     72.     while (dH < -3.14159f) dH += 6.28318f;
2026-03-15T18:19:48.6084227Z     73.     float absDH = dH < 0.0f ? -dH : dH;
2026-03-15T18:19:48.6084492Z     74. 
2026-03-15T18:19:48.6084680Z     75.     float mult;

2026-03-15T18:19:48.6086603Z     80.                (WRONG_DIR_THRESHOLD_RAD - MISALIGNED_THRESHOLD_RAD) * CURVE_SPEED_REDUCTION;

2026-03-15T18:19:48.6088329Z     85.     return std::max(ideal, SPEED_MIN);

2026-03-15T18:20:05.3214994Z       // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3215622Z       // AdaptiveSpeed: ajusta velocidade ao angulo da curva.
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3216090Z       //
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3216593Z       // NOTA: FindSpeedMultiplierWithSpeedFromNodes(m_nStraightLineDistance)
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3217421Z       // e inutil para MISSION_43/34: o campo m_nStraightLineDistance fica
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3218131Z       // fixo em 20 (valor minimo constante) nestas missoes, devolvendo sempre
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3218896Z       // mult=1.0 — sem qualquer reducao de velocidade em curvas.
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3219379Z       //
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3219789Z       // FIX: usa a diferenca de heading entre o veiculo e o targetHeading
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3220493Z       // (calculado por ApplyLaneAlignment) como indicador de curvatura:
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3221244Z       //   |dH| <= 0.3 rad  → em reta:    mult=1.0 (velocidade cheia)
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3222109Z       //   0.3 < |dH| <= 1.5 → em curva:  mult linear de 1.0 ate 0.5 (abranda)
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3222862Z       //   |dH| >  1.5 rad  → WRONG_DIR:  mult=0.3 (minimo — sentido contrario)
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3223610Z       // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3224426Z       unsigned char AdaptiveSpeed(CVehicle* veh, float targetHeading, unsigned char baseSpeed)
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3225100Z       {
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3225394Z           if (!veh) return baseSpeed;
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3225756Z       
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3226072Z           float vH    = veh->GetHeading();
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3226496Z           float dH    = targetHeading - vH;
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3226935Z           while (dH >  3.14159f) dH -= 6.28318f;
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3227386Z           while (dH < -3.14159f) dH += 6.28318f;
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3227808Z           float absDH = dH < 0.0f ? -dH : dH;
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3228197Z       
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3228458Z           float mult;
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3228812Z           if (absDH <= MISALIGNED_THRESHOLD_RAD)
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3229469Z               mult = 1.0f;
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3229865Z           else if (absDH <= WRONG_DIR_THRESHOLD_RAD)
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3230407Z               mult = 1.0f - (absDH - MISALIGNED_THRESHOLD_RAD) /
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3231288Z                      (WRONG_DIR_THRESHOLD_RAD - MISALIGNED_THRESHOLD_RAD) * CURVE_SPEED_REDUCTION;
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3232158Z           else
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3232439Z               mult = 0.3f;
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3232747Z       
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3233226Z           auto ideal = static_cast<unsigned char>(static_cast<float>(baseSpeed) * mult);
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3233873Z           return std::max(ideal, SPEED_MIN);
2026-03-15T18:20:05.3234269Z       }

2026-03-15T18:23:57.5341247Z There's a potential issue with the key input flow: INSERT (VK_MENU_OPEN) is processed in HandleKeys before checking if the menu is open, so pressing INSERT toggles g_menuOpen and returns early. On the next frame, HandleMenuKeys gets called since g_menuOpen is now true, but I need to make sure the state transitions work correctly and keys don't get processed twice. The menu blocking other keys is intentional—it forces the user to interact through the menu system. For the dismiss and recruit actions, RIGHT arrow or ENTER on dismiss closes the menu and executes the action, while recruit just shows a reminder to close the menu first and press the key. I'm reconsidering whether ENTER on recruit should also close the menu and spawn, but keeping it simple with just the label seems cleaner.

According to the updated comment, passing `nullptr` for `ped` is now valid and intentional (affects all members). However, this creates an inconsistency: callers may still pass a valid `ped` pointer expecting member-specific behavior, but the function will now process all members when `ped` is nullptr. Consider adding documentation or validation to ensure callers understand that passing nullptr has group-wide effects, and that passing a specific ped only updates that ped's slot.
2026-03-15T18:26:22.2259026Z     - In grove_recruit_asi/teste/source/grove_recruit_shared.h, lines 211-212: Using `operator new` directly without a corresponding `delete` can lead to memory leaks if the task system doesn't properly manage ownership. The allocated memory is passed to `SetTask` which should take ownership, but this isn't explicitly documented. Consider using `new CTaskComplexBeInGroup(...)` directly if the constructor size is known, or add a comment documenting that `SetTask` takes ownership and will call the destructor/delete when the task is cleared.
2026-03-15T18:26:22.2262698Z     - In grove_recruit_asi/teste/source/grove_recruit_group.cpp, lines 184-186: The flag `bKeepTasksAfterCleanUp` is temporarily set to 0 before `MakeThisPedJoinOurGroup` and then restored to 1 after success at line 195. However, if the re-join fails (lines 201-204), the flag is restored at line 202 but the `AddFollower` fallback is used. This creates inconsistent state: the fallback path doesn't call `EnsureBeInGroup`, so the ped may be in a broken state. Consider calling `EnsureBeInGroup` in the failure path as well to maintain consistency.
2026-03-15T18:26:22.2265940Z     - In grove_recruit_asi/teste/source/grove_recruit_group.cpp, line 426: The compaction loop copies elements but doesn't explicitly clear the source slots during the copy. While the subsequent `while` loop (lines 428-429) clears trailing slots, if `write` ends up equal to `read` for all iterations, no clearing happens. Consider explicitly clearing `g_allRecruits[read]` after copying to ensure no dangling references remain, or add a comment explaining why this is safe.
2026-03-15T18:26:22.2268926Z     - In grove_recruit_asi/teste/source/grove_recruit_menu.cpp, line 256: The menu item label 'Dispensar [1/>>]' suggests that both key '1' and RIGHT arrow trigger dismiss, but according to the code (lines 148-154), only RIGHT arrow triggers dismiss when this item is selected. Key '1' is handled globally in `HandleKeys` (Main.cpp) and calls `DismissRecruit` regardless of menu state. This label is misleading. Consider using `std::max(baseSpeed, SPEED_CIVICO_HIGH)` or capping `effectiveBase` to `baseSpeed` when in degraded modes to maintain safety margins during invalid link recovery.

This could cause the recruit to stand idle if the player enters a vehicle during spawn. Consider adding logic to resume the burst timer when the player exits the vehicle, or document this as intended behavior.
2026-03-15T18:26:22.2295910Z     - In grove_recruit_asi/teste/source/Main.cpp, lines 351-352: The mode change key (4) now only applies `SetupDriveMode` when in DRIVING or PASSENGER states. If the player changes mode while on foot and then enters a vehicle, the mode will be applied. This is likely intended, but consider adding a message or log indicating 'Mode will apply when driving' for states other than DRIVING/PASSENGER to avoid user confusion.

2026-03-15T18:28:58.9744803Z

2026-03-15T18:28:58.9747304Z 
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9748023Z ## Resumo das Mudanças
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9748353Z 
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9748630Z ### 1. Compatibilidade Vanilla (recrutas normais do GTA SA)
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9749854Z **`grove_recruit_group.cpp`** — `ScanPlayerGroup()`:
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9750438Z - Roda a cada 3s (180 frames), varre o grupo do jogador
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9751215Z - Detecta membros recrutados pelo método vanilla (tecla Y + respeito)
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9752684Z - Aplica `bNeverLeavesGroup=1`, `bKeepTasksAfterCleanUp=1`, bit de respeito (`m_acquaintance`) e dá arma se necessário
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9754388Z - Se o mod estiver INACTIVE e houver um recruta vanilla, promove-o a recruta primário automaticamente
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9755014Z 
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9755184Z ### 2. Multi-Recruta (todos entram no carro)
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9756203Z **`grove_recruit_group.cpp`** — `OnPlayerEnterVehicle()` / `OnPlayerExitVehicle()`:
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9759369Z - Quando jogador entra num carro → activa `SIT_IN_LEADER_CAR` (allocator tipo 4): **todos os membros do grupo** tentam entrar no carro do jogador (comportamento vanilla do GTA SA)
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9760667Z - Quando jogador sai → restaura `FOLLOW_LIMITED` (tipo 1)
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9761346Z - `g_allRecruits[7]` rastreia todos os peds (spawned + vanilla), marcados como `isVanilla`
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9762067Z 
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9762207Z ### 3. Menu In-game
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9762542Z **`grove_recruit_menu.cpp`** (ficheiro novo):
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9763020Z - **INSERT** — abre/fecha menu
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9763652Z - **↑/↓** — navegar pelos itens
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9764174Z - **←/→** — alterar modo, aggro, drive-by; confirmar dismiss/fechar
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9764677Z - **ESC** — fechar menu
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9765141Z - Renderizado via `CFont::PrintString` em `Events::drawHudEvent`
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9766050Z - Mostra estado actual, número de recrutas (total/vanilla), modo, aggro, drive-by
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9766546Z 
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9766721Z ### 4. Novos Modos de Condução
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9767582Z - **CIVICO_H** (4): `MC_FOLLOWCAR_FARAWAY(52) + AVOID_CARS` — melhor combinação E+G, segue trajecto do jogador desviando do tráfego
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9768762Z - **CIVICO_I** (5): `MC_ESCORT_REAR_FARAWAY(67) + SLOW_DOWN_FOR_CARS` — travagem suave, bom para estradas com pouco tráfego
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9769535Z - Total: 8 modos (CIVICO_D/E/F/G/H/I + DIRETO + PARADO)
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9769860Z 
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9770011Z ### 5. Melhorias de Velocidade e Curvas
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9770495Z - `SPEED_CIVICO`: 38 → **46 km/h**
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9771337Z - `SPEED_CIVICO_HIGH`: **55 km/h** em retas (|dH| ≤ 0.3 rad) — eliminando a queixa de "muito lento nas retas"
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9772379Z - Protecção: não usa HIGH speed quando `baseSpeed=SPEED_SLOW` (linkId inválido)
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9772809Z 
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9772924Z ### 6. Logging Melhorado
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9773353Z - Categorias novas: `[RECR ]` (multi-recruit/vanilla) e `[MENU ]`
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9774360Z - Observer: distingue membros "mod" vs "vanilla", conta rastreados, linha `RecruitVsNPC` para comparação directa com NPC de tráfego
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9775421Z - Header do log actualizado com documentação de todos os modos e mecanismos
2026-03-15T18:28:58.9775870Z

2026-03-15T18:29:23.8632278Z - No `STAT_RESPECT` manipulation — respects game progression.
2026-03-15T18:29:23.8632643Z

2026-03-15T18:29:23.8633959Z - `OnPlayerEnterVehicle()` activates allocator type `SIT_IN_LEADER_CAR` (4) → all group members attempt to enter player's vehicle using the engine's native mechanism.
2026-03-15T18:29:23.8634960Z - `OnPlayerExitVehicle()` restores `FOLLOW_LIMITED` (1) for on-foot formation.
2026-03-15T18:29:23.8635787Z - `g_allRecruits[7]` tracks all peds (mod-spawned + vanilla), tagged with `isVanilla`.
